[30;1m294 | [0m[35m        # values, so we cannot tell if `point_empty` is really "empty"[0m
[30;1m295 | [0m[35m        # (i.e. unset, like `Point()`) or is just a point at the center[0m
[30;1m296 | [0m[35m        # (which is obviously not "empty"). That's why on the next line[0m
[30;1m297 | [0m[35m        # we assume that `point_empty` is not in the `empty_values` list.[0m
[30;1m298 | [0m[35m        self.assertFalse(point_empty in empty_values)[0m
